msg:During the holidays, I took my family to visit Yancheng Zoo. I saw that this Sheraton was very close and it was a five-star hotel. Although it was expensive and cost more than 1,000 yuan for the room, I thought that I should eat well, drink well and have fun when I went out to play. I never thought that this hotel was really bad and did not live up to its reputation of being a five-star hotel:
1. Service attitude: I booked an executive garden view king room and confirmed by phone that the room was facing the lake and was very quiet. As a result, the front desk gave me a room perpendicular to the lake, but the window could only see half of it. I immediately called the customer service number to complain and they changed me to a proper room;
2. Environment: Maybe the hotel has been renovated for a long time, it is a bit old, which is acceptable I understand, but you can't make it so dirty. There are paper scraps on the carpet, and it is visibly dirty. I dare not use the bathtub. In the end, I spent 10 yuan to buy a bathtub cover. The free fruit is also a rip-off. One of them is rotten.
3. Air conditioning: I will talk about this separately. The temperature is more than 20 during the day, and it is a bit hot when sleeping at night. I want to turn on the air conditioning, but the air conditioning can only adjust the wind speed. The temperature does not work. Finally, I opened the balcony window to cool down. Later, I read the hotel reviews and found that I was not the only one who encountered this problem. It seems to be an old problem.
4. Catering: To be honest, the breakfast is pretty good and worthy of this five-star title;

msg:I went to Yancheng Wildlife Park during the May Day holiday, and I chose the Sheraton Hotel, which is closer, only 5 minutes away by car.
The prices of all hotels during the holidays have risen, but the experience of staying this time is still worth the money.

„Äêcheck in„Äë
Follow the navigation to the hotel and park the car in the underground parking garage. There is no charge for parking.
Came to the L floor, queued for a while, checked in, and the deposit was 1000.
There are quite a variety of welcome fruits, because the children are very happy because they brought some small toys with them.

„Äêenvironment„Äë
The hotel is very big, the lobby bar is spacious and comfortable, and the piano plays beautiful music automatically.
Ctrip users will receive 2 cups of Starbucks coffee when they check in, and they can pick it up at the lobby bar.
The hotel focuses on flower language gardens, the back garden is very beautiful in Chinese style, and there are cozy black swans in the lake.

„Äêfacility„Äë
The decoration facilities of the room are a bit old, after all, the year of decoration is there, but the sanitary condition is still good.
The executive suite I stayed in was very large, with double balconies, two washrooms, wet and dry separation and a large bathtub, and the bed was very comfortable.
Staying guests can use the swimming pool (7:00-22:00) and gym (24 hours) for free.

„ÄêParent-child„Äë
1. Provide children's exclusive toiletry bag.
2. The hotel has opened parent-child activities. I don‚Äôt know if they are only held on holidays. During the May Day period, there will be one in the morning and one in the afternoon, graffiti, handicrafts, baking, etc.
3. There is also a small children's playground next to the cafeteria, and an outdoor slide playground, which is not too big, but it is also good for children to discharge.
4. The newly renovated 4 immersive parent-child room types, visited a super nice one, the children will definitely be very happy to stay, next time we have the opportunity to come, we will choose this room.
5. The 3 robots in the lobby are the most popular among children. Many children follow behind and run around. You can also let the robots deliver food directly to the room.

„ÄêServe„Äë
1. There are a lot of concierge staff, answering every question, very polite and professional.
2. The best impression is that Nico, the housekeeper I met when I checked in, was very professional and enthusiastic. He sent us to the room, helped us with our luggage, and introduced various facilities of the hotel along the way. Later, during the check-in, he also actively asked Are you satisfied with the check-in, did you sleep well, did you eat the buffet breakfast, it feels so kind, and she also helped us apply for a late check-out, special thanks to her!
3. It happened to be my birthday on the day I checked in. When we came back from playing, I was very surprised to see a big cake with a towel on the bed.

„ÄêFOOD„Äë
The buffet breakfast (07:00-10:00) is quite satisfactory, with everything you need, Chinese food and Western food are good, and the small wontons and silver noodles are super delicious!
I prefer the executive lounge (17:30-19:30), the dining environment is quieter, although there are not many dishes, but I have been there for 2 days, and they are very appetizing.
On the first floor of the hotel, there are also options for buffet dinner, Cantonese cuisine, Japanese cuisine, etc., and the hotel can also provide outdoor camping barbecues.

So in general, Marriott's hotels are still very trustworthy, and the stay is also very happy, recommended!
